# Comments for Question 4, LLM=Claude Sonnet 4 (no reasoning)

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=7.9)
    The story effectively explores themes of memory, impermanence, and creation as resistance to oblivion. The bee pin serves as a powerful symbol that transitions from representing loss to possibility. The narrative skillfully shows rather than tells emotional development, particularly in Geth's journey from protective isolation to vulnerable connection. The ending resonates with hopeful possibility. However, some metaphors ("weathered heart") are repeated rather than developed with fresh variations.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=7.5)
    The story effectively contrasts perfection versus imperfection through the parallel between dueling and cooking, with strong metaphorical resonance. The grandmother's inscription provides a powerful emotional catalyst. However, some telling rather than showing ("his throat tightened") and occasional purple prose diminish the impact. The central theme is compelling but could benefit from more subtle development rather than explicit statements.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=7.8)
    The story effectively uses the net as both physical object and metaphor for liberation, with untying knots paralleling psychological release. The "mundanely spiritual" theme maintains consistent tension throughout. While the emotional impact is strong, the story occasionally tells rather than shows ("Marcus understood why"). The ending achieves poignancy through the transformation of both character and object, leaving readers with the powerful image of carrying "the fisherman's patience."

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=7.3)
    The story effectively explores themes of complicity, redemption, and the ethics of guardianship. The pressed pennies as physical manifestations of stolen dreams is a strong metaphorical device. While the narrative creates intrigue and some emotional resonance, the resolution feels somewhat hasty, and the dialogue occasionally states themes too directly rather than revealing them through action.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.5)
